[35m│[0m                                                                                                                                                                                           [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92mCRITICAL - CONTEXT TRACKING:[0m                                                                                                                                                             [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- If question refers to "that", "it", "this value" → use MOST RECENT calculation result from history[0m                                                                                     [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- For "what is that less 1?" → subtract(previous_result, 1)[0m                                                                                                                              [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- For "what is that times 100?" → multiply(previous_result, 100)[0m                                                                                                                         [35m│[0m

[35m│[0m  [92mCRITICAL - SPECIAL QUESTION PATTERNS:[0m                                                                                                                                                    [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- "percentage change" → "divide(subtract(new_value, old_value), old_value)"[0m                                                                                                              [35m│[0m

[35m│[0m  [92m- "difference between A and B" → "subtract(A, B)" (be careful with order!)[0m                                                                                                               [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- "change from X to Y" → "subtract(Y, X)"[0m                                                                                                                                                [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- "what is that less 1" → "subtract(previous_result, 1)"[0m                                                                                                                                 [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m                                                                                                                                                                                           [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92mEXAMPLES:[0m                                                                                                                                                                                [35m│[0m
